The Yayue Society Will Hold a Music Concert

The local Yayue Society was originally organized by young men and women in our country, with more than 60 members. Every winter solstice, there would be a music concert at the City Hall on Nanjing Road. The proceeds from the ticket sales would be used to fund the society and to help charity. Last year, due to the reconstruction of the City Hall into a shopping mall, it was difficult to find a suitable location to hold the regular meeting. It is now learned that they have rented the Beijing Grand Theatre and are planning to perform on a selected date. The members of the society are all very excited and are actively preparing. At that time, there will be high songs and dances, and the place will be bustling with carriages and horses, it will surely be a grand occasion.

Female Teacher's Case Against Foreman for Enticement to be Sentenced

▲Ni Xiuzhen Invites Luo Cuiyu to Testify

▲Zhu Haisheng Denies Having a Child with Ni

▲The Sentence in this Case is Scheduled for the 27th

The female teacher Ni Xiuzhen sued the foreman of the Ruiyong Iron Factory, Zhu Haisheng, for the crime of enticement and abduction in the Special District Court. Subsequently, she lost the case and appealed to the High Court. The case has been heard three times, and all the details have been reported in previous newspapers. Yesterday afternoon, the hearing date arrived again, and witnesses were summoned to testify. At 4:30 p.m., Judge Song opened the first court to hear the case. Ni Xiuzhen and her mother, Ni Zhongshi, and Zhu Haisheng all arrived in court on time to await questioning. The hearing proceeded as follows:

▲Ni Xiuzhen Judge Song first (asked) Ni Xiuzhen, "Has the witness Zhang Guangpei arrived?" Ni (replied), "Zhang and his wife have gone to Nanjing to work, so they are not here today. But Luo Baoshan's wife, who lives with me, is willing to testify in court. Mrs. Luo has arrived, please summon (her)."

▲Luo Cuiyu The witness Luo Cuiyu was summoned to the witness stand and stated, "I live with Ni Xiuzhen at No. 9 Qingdao Road. The house is a three-story building with about three or four tenants. I live on the upper floor of the east wing, the landlord lives downstairs, and the upper floor of the living room is where Zhu Haisheng and Ni Xiuzhen lived." Judge Song (asked), "Did Ni Zhongshi often come?" (Answered), "She came when Xiuzhen's son had his one-month celebration." (Asked), "What day was the one-month celebration?" (Answered), "June 18th last year." (Asked), "When did you move out?" (Answered), "Roughly when the house was demolished, but I have forgotten the date." (Asked), "Do you know Ni Zhongshi?" (Answered), "I only met her at the one-month celebration. I had never seen her before."

▲Ni Zhongshi Judge Song then summoned Ni Zhongshi (asked), "When did you move into No. 9 Qingdao Road?" (Answered), "August 3rd of the 19th year." (Asked), "Did your daughter rent the room before or after you?" (Answered), "Xiuzhen rented in April, I rented in August." (Asked), "How did you know about Ni Xiuzhen and Zhu Haisheng's affair?" (Answered), "In December of the 18th year, I saw that she was pregnant. After questioning her, I learned the truth. After learning about this, I wanted Zhu to marry her because what's done is done. However, Zhu's parents had to come forward for a formal marriage, because my husband used to work as a translator in the police station, and naturally, I did not want my daughter to be someone's mistress." (Asked), "Did you go to No. 9 when your grandson had his one-month celebration?" (Answered), "I never went."

▲Zhu Haisheng Judge Song then summoned Zhu Haisheng (asked), "What exactly happened between you and Ni Xiuzhen from beginning to end?" (Answered), "After meeting Ni Xiuzhen upstairs in the Yong'an Company in February of the 16th year, I went to her house to play cards. At this time, she and Ni Zhongshi were already living on Qingdao Road. Ni Zhongshi knew about my affair with her daughter a long time ago. I stopped going there in the second half of the 18th year. The house at No. 9 Qingdao Road was not rented by me, and I do not know the witness either." (Asked), "You stopped going there in the 18th year, so why did Ni Xiuzhen have a child in the 19th year?" (Answered), "That is their nonsense. I did not have a child with her." (Asked), "How much money did you spend in total?" (Answered), "About a thousand yuan."

▲Sentencing Date At this point, the lawyers for both sides, Qiu Fenling and Ye Fokang, argued vigorously. After the arguments, Judge Song announced that the debate in this case was concluded and that the sentence would be pronounced at 2:00 p.m. on the 27th. Zhu Haisheng was detained.

Attempted Kidnapping Mistook Aunt

▲What's Done is Done

Chen Fulan, a farmer near Ruizhi Bridge in Northwest Wusong, has two daughters, the elder named Aizhen, aged twenty, and the younger named Aiyun, aged seventeen. Both are beautiful and of similar height and build, almost identical. Both daughters had been betrothed since childhood. Aizhen was betrothed to a son of the Zhang family in Jiangwan, but she became a widow before marriage (commonly known as a widow of the door). Aiyun was betrothed to Zou Yuexiang, the son of Zou Wangshi, a neighboring farmer. Zou is twenty-one years old and comes from a very poor family, so he has no means to marry. Last year, Zou repeatedly asked a matchmaker to intercede with the Chen family, intending to marry hastily to start a family. However, the Chen family, due to the poverty of the Zou family, not only refused the request but also had intentions of breaking the engagement. Upon receiving this news, Zou Yuexiang was extremely distressed. Later, in September of last year, Zou, encouraged by friends and relatives, gathered many people and went to the Chen family to kidnap the bride. Because the Chen family had heard rumors beforehand, the whole family hid, so the incident did not succeed. Afterwards, the Chen family became strictly vigilant, and Zou Yuexiang gave up due to lack of ideas. Until 3 p.m. the day before yesterday, the Chen family had forgotten about the previous incident. As it was the Lunar New Year, Aizhen and Aiyun, dressed in new clothes, went out for a stroll. On the way, they happened to meet Zou Yuexiang. Seeing an opportunity, Zou immediately ran back home and gathered many friends and relatives to follow them and attempt a second kidnapping. Seeing the situation was bad, Chen Aizhen asked her sister to hide quickly. When Zou and the others arrived, they only saw Aizhen walking on the road. Because Aizhen looked very similar to Aiyun, Zou and the others, without distinguishing between right and wrong, kidnapped Aizhen to their home. Although Aizhen argued that she was not the one they wanted, the Zou family did not believe her and immediately forced Aizhen to worship the ancestors and get married with Yuexiang, and they shared the same bed. When Aiyun escaped home and told her father, Chen Lanfu, Chen did not think the Zou family would kidnap his elder daughter, so he dismissed it. It was not until late in the evening when Aizhen had not returned home that he knew something was wrong. He rushed to the Zou family, but it was already too late. Yesterday morning, Chen, along with the original matchmaker and many friends and relatives, went to the Zou family to negotiate. The two sides almost resorted to violence. Unexpectedly, something unexpected happened. Aizhen, having been mistakenly kidnapped by the Zou family, saw that Zou Yuexiang did not look too bad, so she told him that she was willing to serve him. When she saw her father coming to negotiate, she came out and begged her father to calm down and take a long-term view. Chen, as what's done is done, could only sigh helplessly. After mediation by relatives and friends of both sides, it was agreed that Aizhen would marry into the Zou family, Aiyun would be re-engaged to someone else, and the Zou family would pay fifty yuan and hold a banquet on a scheduled date to entertain the friends and relatives of both the Chen and Zou families, and kowtow to Chen Fulan in public to apologize, as a settlement.

Change of Ownership of the 大陆报

▲Four Chinese and Four Foreigners in the New Board of Directors

The 美大晚报 reported: "The local English 大陆报 was founded in 1911. Mr. Miller, currently serving as an advisor to the National Government, was the editor at the time. At that time, the newspaper was owned by Americans, and its reporters and staff were all American. After several years, it was purchased by Mr. Isla, the late owner of the British Jardine Matheson & Co. After Mr. Isla passed away, it was taken over by Isla's wife. Now, Mr. Dong Xianguang, representing merchants from Shanghai and North China, has purchased it. The price and the names of the new owners have not been released. Mr. Dong is currently the general manager of the newspaper. It was stated yesterday that the new board of directors consists of four Chinese and four foreigners. He is also one of the Chinese directors. The chairman of the board is Mr. Heckmond, a well-known American lawyer in Shanghai. The newspaper will continue to be a company registered in the United States. It is currently planning to hire news experts to make major improvements to increase the interest of readers. The newspaper's editorial department has moved to No. 36 Sichuan Road. The business department, currently located at No. 14.5 Jiujiang Road, will also be relocated soon. It is also heard that the new company will choose a site to build its own building."

Modification Completed on First and Second City Ferries

▲Inspected and Accepted Respectively on the Previous Two Days

The City Public Works Bureau built the No. 1 and No. 2 ferries in November of the 18th year and January of the 19th year respectively. Since their launch, a year has passed. According to customs regulations, repairs were necessary. The bureau, due to the completion of the No. 3 and No. 4 ferries in December of last year, which were capable of replacing the original ferries, submitted a request to the municipal government to have the No. 1 and No. 2 ferries repaired by the He Xing Machinery Manufacturing Factory and to expand the cabin space. Now that the work has been completed, the municipal government sent Counselor Xi Dingmo, together with Bureau Chief Huang, to inspect and accept the ferries at 2:00 PM on the 19th and 20th of this month, respectively. It is reported that the two ferries have been newly painted after the repairs. The middle layer, originally divided into special and first-class cabins, has now been entirely expanded into first-class cabins, with the special class cabins moved to the upper layer. Therefore, the capacity has increased, which is sufficient to meet the needs after the extension of the route to Gaoqiao. In addition, it is reported that the three cross-river ferries ordered by the bureau in August of last year were also inspected and accepted by Counselor Xi on the 13th of this month. The opening of the cross-river ferry service is not far off.

Wife of Thief/Bandit Conceals Firearms

▲Related to the Gunshot Wound of a Constable Case

Cao Zhixiu from Xuzhou, on the evening of the 27th of last month, specially invited Du Chengsong from Haizhou and others to his home to secretly discuss robbing a foreign goods store at No. 478 Huade Road. Cao's wife, Wang, was responsible for providing firearms. At 8:00 PM that night, Wang hid a handgun on her person and went to the store first, claiming to buy foreign cloth. The shop assistant, unaware of their scheme, was showing her the goods to choose from when Cao, Du, and other thieves swarmed into the store. Wang immediately took out the handgun and robbed the store, looting their fill and escaping. Afterwards, the shop owner, Chen Guoliang, filed a report with the Huishan Police Station, stating that the total value of the lost property was 338 yuan, and requested an investigation. Subsequently, detectives Shi Huanjing, Liu Baoshan, Zhao Rongsheng, and others arrested Cao, Wang, and another man, three in total. Under investigation, it was discovered that the case of the Tianyi Printing Company on Bei'er Road being broken into on August 20th last year at 11:00 AM, although the robbery was unsuccessful, and the gatekeeper constable, Lu Huaxing, was shot in the foot by the thieves, was also committed by Cao and others. The constable was summoned to the police station to identify the suspects. According to him, Cao was indeed present at the scene, holding a handgun and firing three shots, resulting in the constable being wounded in the foot. Based on his testimony, the police station added a charge of attempted robbery and a charge of shooting and wounding the constable against Cao Zhixiu. Yesterday morning, the colleagues were summoned to bring the three men and women to the Special District Local Court, where Judge Feng interrogated them. The constable suddenly identified Du Chengsong as one of the thieves present at the scene. When questioned, both Cao and Du confessed to the Huade Road case. However, their statements regarding the Tianyi Printing Company robbery attempt and the shooting of the constable were ambiguous. Cao's wife, Wang, also stubbornly denied everything, claiming that Du's statement that she carried the handgun as a pretext to buy cloth at the store was false. After Judge Feng finished recording the statements, he ordered the defendants to be detained separately, awaiting sentencing at a later date.

Two Thieves Heavily Sentenced in Two Concessions

The two bandits, Zhou Agou and Qian Zhengxiang, colluded with a gang to rob the old clerk of Baoda Xiang Foreign Goods Store on Tongyun Street outside the Xiaodongmen in the French Concession on September 13th of last year, stealing several thousand silver dollars, resisted arrest with gunfire, and fled with the loot. The victim reported the case to the police station and requested their arrest. Now, Zhou and Qian have committed crimes in the British Concession and were recently arrested. They were sent to the Special District Court, where Zhou was sentenced to 11 years and Qian to 16 years. Now, detective Zeng Jiuru and Bao detective Liu Jinrong of the French Police Station have learned of this and went to retrieve Zhou and Qian from the British Concession. Yesterday, they were sent to the French Court for questioning. The plaintiff first recounted the previous incident. Zhou and Qian confessed to the robbery. The Chinese and Western judges sentenced Zhou and Qian to five years in the Western prison each, followed by deportation and transfer to the inland authorities for further investigation.

Seducing and Raping a Neighbor's Adopted Daughter

▲Chen Huihong Cannot Deny the Charges

Liu Longgen, the 16-year-old adopted daughter of Teng Kaifu, a Yangzhou native residing at No. 77 Nanxing Road, Datong Road, Zhabei, disappeared while playing at the door at 6:30 PM on the 18th of this month. Teng immediately asked relatives and friends to search for her and investigated various hotels. Until 7:20 AM the next morning (the 19th), while passing the entrance of the Aiwen Hotel at No. 1892 Aiwenyi Road in the Public Concession, he saw Chen Huihong (age 20), a native of Yuyao, walking out of the hotel. Chen also lived on Nanxing Road, opposite Teng's residence, and they had seen each other before. Suspecting Chen of being involved in the adopted daughter's disappearance, Teng immediately grabbed him. Chen admitted that Liu Longgen had indeed stayed overnight with him in the hotel and led Teng to room 39, where they found Longgen getting out of bed. They immediately called constable No. 177 and Chinese detective Weng Peiyu, who arrested Chen and took him to the Xin Zha Police Station. The girl was sent to the hospital, where it was confirmed that she had been raped. Yesterday morning, Chen was sent to the Second Criminal Court of the Special District Local Court. Zhang Tianyin, the police station's lawyer, presented the case, stating that the police station was prosecuting Chen for the crime of raping a girl under the age of sixteen under Article 240, Section 2 of the Criminal Law, and requested punishment. The examination report was also submitted for review. Teng Kaifu stated that although his adopted daughter was sixteen years old, she was born on December 12th and was therefore only fifteen years old. She was not yet married to his son. He also recounted the circumstances of her disappearance. The girl, Liu Longgen, also testified that she was sixteen years old and had been adopted into the Teng family at the age of twelve, but was not yet married. She had been working in a silk factory and had known the defendant since June of last year. Chen invited her to see a movie at the Zhabei Grand Theater at 6:00 PM the day before yesterday. Before the movie was over, Chen lured her to the Aiwen Hotel. Upon arriving at the entrance, they met Wu Shizhen and entered room 39 together. Soon after, Chen took a cotton robe to the pawnshop. Wu was watching her while Chen pawned the robe for eight yuan, and then Wu left. Around 8:00 PM, she was forcibly raped by Chen. She was only found by her father the next morning, and so on. The defendant claimed that he lived in the cigarette paper shop opposite the plaintiff's residence and that he had known Liu since she came to buy things, which had been about ten months. They had gone to the movies several times together. The day before yesterday, Liu went to the Zhabei Grand Theater to see a movie with a young girl and Wu Shizhen. At that time, Liu claimed that she did not want to go home, so she stayed with him. After Judge Ge Zhitan examined the testimony, he ordered a court attendant to take Liu to the forensic medical office for another examination. It was determined that Liu's hymen was newly broken. The court then appointed Wang Weizhen as the defendant's lawyer and ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody, awaiting sentencing on the 27th of this month.

Car Collision Kills a Woman

Kong, the wife of Zhang Yangao from Suzhou, was walking from east to west on Aidaoya Road at 10:30 PM on the 6th of this month when she turned onto Songshan Road. A car with license plate number 7194 was speeding towards her, and they could not avoid each other. Kong was knocked down and seriously injured. Patrol officers took the injured woman to Renji Hospital for treatment and identified her husband, who lived at No. 591 Zhaojia Road, Ximen, and notified Zhang Yangao to go to the hospital. The driver, Chen Xingsheng, was summoned to the police station for questioning and ordered to wait for instructions. However, Kong's injuries were critical, and she died in the hospital the day before yesterday. Her body was taken to the Feilun Road morgue. Yesterday morning, the husband and the driver were summoned. The Special District Local Court appointed Prosecutor Guo to inspect the body. According to Chen Xingsheng, the deceased was crossing the road at the time and was not careful, which was not due to his negligent driving. Zhang Yangao, the husband, requested that the examination be waived so that he could prepare the coffin. Prosecutor Guo approved the request, ordered Zhang to sign a guarantee, and allowed him to claim the body.

New Regulations for Issuing Passports for Going Abroad

▲Implemented Starting Yesterday

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs, based on the Central Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission's consultation, stated that overseas Chinese merchants had repeatedly complained that the fees for Chinese passports for going abroad and passports for passing through territories were too high and the validity period was too short. They requested that new regulations be revised to benefit overseas Chinese. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs stated that for passports for passing through territories, such as going to Yunnan, which required passing through Vietnam, and Xinjiang, which required passing through the Siberian Railway, these passports belonged to domestic travel and should be charged half the fee. This had been consulted by the Shanghai Municipal Government and informed the Municipal Public Security Bureau to comply. Now, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has reduced the fees for Chinese passports for going abroad and extended the validity period. The new regulations have been submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval and promulgation. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has consulted the Shanghai Municipal Government and the Municipal and County Governments regarding the approved new regulations, and instructed the passport-issuing authorities to comply with them. It is reported that after receiving the order, the Municipal Public Security Bureau immediately rushed to print the new regulations and sent them to various public groups. Starting yesterday (the 20th), the new regulations and the new passports issued by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs have been implemented.

▲Investigating the Situation of the Chinese Press

Important Announcement from the Hydrographic Office

▲The Location of the Dark Reef in Tongzhou Sand has been Surveyed Accurately

▲The Coastal Area of Our Country has been Divided

▲Mooring Buoys Near Shanghai Harbor Have Been Added and Modified

The Naval Hydrographic Office has issued three important announcements as follows:

A. The exact location of the dark reef in the Tongzhou Sand of the Yangtze River on the coast of the Republic of China has now been accurately surveyed: (Location) 291 degrees true north from the Wolf Mountain Pagoda, a distance of 5.77 nautical miles, 120 degrees 46 minutes 33 seconds east longitude, 31 degrees 59 minutes 12 seconds north latitude; (Depth) can be level with the lowest tide level.

The applicable symbol is indicated on the chart. (Description) Extends half a cable length to the north (each ten cable lengths equal one nautical mile), two cable lengths to the east, half a cable length to the south, and one cable length to the west. Within this range, the water depth does not exceed six English feet. (Note) The four boundaries of the reef are surrounded by a curved danger line and named Qingtian Reef.

B. The coastal areas of the Republic of China are divided as follows: (South Coast of the Republic of China) From the border between the Republic of China and French Indochina to Yamen and the mouth of the West River in Guangdong is one section; (Southeast Coast) From Yamen and the mouth of the West River in Guangdong to Pinghai in Fujian is one section; (East Coast) From Pinghai in Fujian to Haimenzui (the eastern end of the left bank of the Yangtze River) in Jiangsu is one section; (Northeast Coast) From Haimenzui (the eastern end of the left bank of the Yangtze River) in Jiangsu to Shandong Cape is one section; (North Coast) From Shandong Cape to the border between the Republic of China and Korea is one section, including the Bohai Bay and the Liaodong Bay.

C. Mooring buoys in the Shanghai port of the Yangtze River: relocation and increase: (Location) Upper section A of the Shanghai port, the flagpole of the naval flag station inside the Jiangnan Shipyard (hereinafter referred to as the flagpole) is at 121 degrees 29 minutes east longitude, 31 degrees 11 minutes 44.9 seconds north latitude; (Fourth buoy in the center of the river) 212 degrees true north from the flagpole, a distance of 2.15 cable lengths; (Fifth buoy) 224 degrees true north from the flagpole, a distance of 2.92 cable lengths; (Sixth buoy) 233 degrees true north from the flagpole, a distance of 3.92 cable lengths; (Seventh buoy) 237.5 degrees true north from the flagpole, a distance of 4.73 cable lengths. The buoys near the Huangpu River (No. 1) 240.5 degrees true north from the flagpole, a distance of 2.2 cable lengths; (No. 2) Remains in its original location; (No. 3) 245.5 degrees true north from the flagpole, a distance of 3.29 cable lengths; (No. 4) 247 degrees true north from the flagpole, a distance of 3.78 cable lengths; (No. 5) 247.5 degrees true north from the flagpole, a distance of 4.3 cable lengths.

Social Affairs Bureau Recruiting Weights and Measures Inspectors

▲Exam Dates: 25th and 26th

The City Social Affairs Bureau was ordered to prepare for the establishment of a weights and measures inspection office, which has already been established. All personnel in the office are recruited by the bureau and sent to Beijing for studies. After three months, they will return to Shanghai to take up their positions. As the deadline for standardization is approaching, the workload of the office is heavy, and the original staff is insufficient. Therefore, the bureau submitted a request to the municipal government to continue recruiting five second-class inspectors to be sent to the Weights and Measures Inspection Personnel Training Institute of the Ministry of Industry for studies. After completing their studies, they will return to the office to take up their positions with a monthly salary of 60 yuan, which will increase annually based on their work diligence. A travel allowance of 30 yuan will be given once during the period of study at the ministry. Registration has already begun, and the exam dates are set for the 25th and 26th. Graduates of senior high schools, university preparatory courses, old-system Class A vocational schools, or old-system middle schools with certificates are eligible to apply. The exam subjects are Party principles, Chinese language, English language, mathematics (arithmetic, algebra, geometry, trigonometry), physics, chemistry, the use of weights and measures, and oral examination. It is reported that many people have gone to the bureau to register in recent days.

The police station found that Xu had fire insurance of 5,000 taels, so he was summoned to the French Court for questioning yesterday. The chief first reported the previous situation. Verdict on the Fujian Maru Kidnapping Case

Relief society investigators Chen Shaoting and Lin Yongfang recently discovered kidnappers Ren Chengwu, Huang Qingzhen, Lin Junchu, and the female kidnapper Lin Liu, as well as kidnapped girls Chen Meifeng and Tan Xia, and boy Zhao Zigui on the Fujian Maru steamship. They were immediately sent to the Local Court, where the prosecutor filed a public prosecution. The Criminal Court concluded the trial yesterday and announced the verdict. Ren Chengwu, Huang Qingzhen, and Lin Yichu were each sentenced to one year in prison. Lin Liu was sentenced to one year and four months as a warning.

Financial Bar Gold Report Rebounds and Soars

Rebounded by Twelve Taels and Eight Mace

Difference of Twenty Taels and Five Cash

▲Conflicting News Leads to Great Fluctuations

Yesterday, February 20th, the price of bar gold rebounded again, and 780 taels had been sent to Guanwai. However, the market situation was bizarre and volatile, and sudden rises and falls of several taels were not uncommon. Although the surging waves were difficult to suppress, the front and rear markets had a total difference of 20 taels. As for foreign exchange, it rebounded by one level, but the internal situation was different, and in the end, the price was tightly raised. The buying and selling in the market were different, and the psychology of each firm was quite uncertain.

Firms such as Yuansheng, Zhifengyong, Hengxingyuan, and Yu Da generally bought in, while Qianchangxiang, Changshengyong, Yuantai, and Hongli advanced and then exited. Hengxing continued to sell off. The overseas silver market rose, and because of the news that Citibank had rescued the silver market, the price of gold opened lower. Afterwards, the buyers showed strong interest, especially because the Sino-US loan may not be successful, which boosted people's confidence and caused the price to soar. After a rise of more than ten taels, Hengxing and Qianchangxiang sold off, because it was rumored that there was a need for cash abroad, which caused the price to plummet. At times, there were plateaus of six or seven taels. At noon, the exchange rate eased, and the sellers on the counter were agile and showed signs of fatigue, falling sharply by more than ten taels to within 75 taels. The after-hours market rebounded to more than 80 taels as Fuchang and Xinheng bought in, but the fluctuations were small, with a review of ten taels. The final price was 83 or 84 taels. The spot market seemed to be active, so the red strip increased by one tael. It is said that the big bar price tended to fall this morning.

▲Big Bar Report Opened Lower

The April opening price in the morning fell by three and a half taels to 767 and a half taels. The big bar price was indeed up 3/16, the silver price was up 5/8, and the private telegram was also up 9/16. Afterwards, Fuchang and Fuyu bought in, and because the US-China loan was still difficult to approach, people's confidence went up and soared. The price soared by more than 13 taels when the shilling opened, reaching 81 taels. The posted price was up 25, the US dollar was up half a yuan, and the Japanese gold was down a small 3/25 and was not moved. However, the internal stability was firm, and Maihang offered May British gold at 1 shilling and 2 pence, which was then bought by HSBC at the same price in April. In addition, Zhifengyong, Dadecheng, Qianchangxiang, Hengxingyuan, and others sold and bought, so the price increased by more than four taels. At 9:30, it was 85 and a half taels. Afterwards, Yuan Maoyong and Hengxing sold off, and it was rumored that there was a need for silver abroad, which lowered people's confidence. The price fell more than seven taels to 78 taels at a little after 10:10. Shortly after, buyers did not slack off, and Yuancheng, Yongheng, and Yuanheng chased in. In addition, Sumitomo and Taiwan bought May British gold at 2 pence, and the hedging firms then put in slips, so the price rose again by six or seven taels, but there were fluctuations of two or three taels at a time, reaching 85 taels at 11:10. Afterwards, Hongli, Changshengyong, Qianchangxiang, and others sold off again. The supply on the counter exceeded demand, making it difficult for the market price to stand firm. In the violent storm, the price fell miserably by twelve taels. The British gold can be settled at 1.20625. Education News

Important News

Ministry of Education Instructions on How Overseas Chinese Students Return to China for Further Education

According to the National Tsinghua University's request for instructions on how overseas Chinese students should return to China for further education, the Ministry of Education approved the Philippine Chinese High School's letter stating that, in order to adapt to the environment, the local schools' academic years are consistent with those of Philippine schools (7 years for primary school and 4 years for secondary school). Upon secondary school graduation, many students plan to return to China for further education at universities. Please send your school's charter and provide instructions on admission procedures. In the future, when taking the entrance examination for your school, what level will they be allowed to take? Are there any preferential policies for overseas Chinese students returning to China? Please provide detailed information. Accordingly, regarding what measures should be taken for overseas Chinese students to return to China for further education after graduating from schools in their current location, our school has no regulations or systems to follow. In light of the school's inquiry, we have requested instructions. The Ministry of Education instructed: "We have received the report. The Overseas Chinese Education Conference convened by the Central Training Department resolved that for national and provincial schools with overseas Chinese children returning to China to study, those who are certified by overseas Chinese organizations as being poor may be granted tuition waivers by the schools based on their circumstances. Overseas Chinese students who are not admitted to the domestic schools they apply to should be directly introduced by the schools to schools of equivalent academic level or attend remedial classes in schools with overseas Chinese remedial classes, or the schools should provide opportunities for remedial classes on their own. This principle should be followed until specific regulations are established for overseas Chinese students returning to China to study. We hereby order you to be informed."

Dr. Dewey to Lecture in China

The North China Daily News reports that the famous American philosopher and educator Dr. Dewey has accepted an invitation from the China Foundation for the Promotion of Education and Culture to come to China to study. Upon arrival, he will lecture at various famous national universities.

Ministry of Education Approves Correction of Old Phonetic Dictionaries

The Ministry of Education, according to the report of Tang Yuezhen, professor of National Wuhan University, Hubei Province, approved the correction of old national phonetic dictionaries (since the National Government has promulgated the new phonetic notation, it seems inappropriate to allow the old national phonetic dictionaries to continue to be sold on the market, which is useless to book buyers and harmful to the future of phonetic notation. It is hoped that measures will be taken to require bookstores that publish this type of old national phonetic dictionary to first correct the old national phonetics in an appropriate manner, and then allow them to be sold freely, otherwise they should be strictly prohibited). The Ministry of Education instructed: "We have received the report. The professor's request is feasible. After the new national phonetic commonly used character collection compiled by the Ministry's National Language Unification Preparation Committee is completed and submitted to the Ministry for promulgation, we will immediately order the bookstores to correct the phonetic notations in the old national phonetic dictionaries, etc., in accordance with the new system, in order to unify them and avoid errors. Please inform them accordingly."

▲ Zhang Ji and Lu Dangping Went North Last Night

Montessori Education Method

▲ Not Applicable to China

丨The Ministry of Education Requests the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to Convey Montessori's Message丨

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs, according to the report of the Italian Embassy, stated that Dr. Montessori sent a book on the Montessori Education Method and five copies of the regulations of the Montessori Education Method Training Institute, as well as a letter to Minister Jiang of the Ministry of Education, requesting that it be forwarded and stating that if there are reports and documents from schools in your country that use the Montessori Education Method, please request the Ministry of Education to send one or two copies. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs forwarded the regulations of the Montessori Education Method Training Institute and Montessori's letter to Minister Jiang to the Ministry of Education for review and reply. The Ministry of Education replied to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs the day before yesterday, attaching a translated copy of Montessori's article and requesting that it be forwarded to Montessori. The main idea of the original letter was: "We previously received Dr. Montessori's letter requesting that personnel be sent to Rome to learn her education method, and we replied and promised to send a Chinese translation of the Montessori Education Method at any time. It has been found that schools in our country have been experimenting with this education method for ten years. At that time, in order to strive to suit the educational principles, Montessori teaching aids were also produced and used. However, according to those who have actually experimented, this method requires too many teaching aids, and each child needs teaching aids worth about 50 yuan, which seems uneconomical and difficult to promote in China. Recently, kindergartens and lower grades of primary schools in various places in China generally use project-based teaching methods, using the living environment and daily sights and sounds as teaching materials, and do not pay much attention to the use of more mechanical special teaching aids. Therefore, for this education method, we only learn its spirit and have no specific experiments to report." In addition to including a book on Montessori and her education, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is requested to forward it to show the Chinese translation of the education method.

The official opening of the semester will be on March 2nd (Monday). The Ministry of Education's office for dispatched takeover committee members will also handle the handover on the 22nd.

Key Points of the National Games Competition Regulations

Nanjing Central Telegraph on the 20th - The National Games competition regulations, consisting of thirty-four articles, have been approved for record. The National Government issued an order on the 20th to instruct the Executive Yuan to forward its key points: (1) The competition period is from October 10th to 20th; (2) The competition is based on provinces, cities, regions, and overseas Chinese groups as units; (3) The qualifications of athletes are citizens of the Republic of China and amateur athletes; (4) There are nine types of championships for men, five for women, and three for national martial arts; (5) The overall championship is divided into two types for men; (7) Each unit should report the types of championships they intend to participate in to the conference before September 19th, and submit the complete list of athletes to the conference before September 25th.

Results of Yesterday's Shanghai Basketball Association Competition

▲ Youth Won Against 33 by 38 to 15

▲ Lively Won Against Tu Jin by 15 to 14

▲ Mei Gong Won Against Huadong by 42 to 30

Among the three groups of games in the Shanghai Basketball Association last night, the game between Mei Gong and Huadong was the most interesting, with about six or seven hundred spectators. The results were: (1) Youth won against Team 33, 38 to 15; (2) Lively won against Tu Jin, 15 to 14; (3) Mei Gong won against Huadong, 42 to 30.

▲ Youth Won Against 33 (Group B1) - The Youth team has outstanding talents, is well-trained, and their movements are clean and graceful. Team 33 was also a strong team, but in comparison, they were far inferior to the Youth team. When the Youth team scored twenty points, Team 33 just started recording. The first half was 22 to 5. Starting in the second half, Team 33 tried to retaliate and made many achievements, making the situation slightly peaceful. As a result, Qing Guang scored 38 points, and Team 33 scored 15 points.

▲ Lively Won Against Tu Jin (Group B2) - The two teams were evenly matched, and the situation was balanced. The score in the first half was 9 to 4, with Lively taking the lead. In the second half, Tu Jin launched a fierce counterattack, and the situation was very tense. Tu Jin once took the lead with 14 to 13, but in the end, Lively won by one point with a score of 15 to 14, which was also very dangerous.

▲ Mei Gong Won Against Huadong (Group A) - Mei Gong's strength is very strong, even better than the West Youth Sea [blank]. They have the greatest hope for the championship of this Shanghai Association. Although Huadong was also famous for a while, they were ultimately not their opponents. In the battle, Ouyang of Huadong scored the first point. From then on, Mei School's momentum was great, and their charge was unstoppable. The performance of Shiguya and Pilei was praised by the audience. Although Huadong also had a good performance, it was difficult to surpass the former, and their defense was overwhelmed. In the first half, Mei Gong scored 21 points, and Huadong scored 8 points. Starting in the second half, the situation was as before. Later, Mei Gong's lineup was adjusted from time to time, and their strength was slightly weaker. Huadong took the opportunity to counterattack, and the momentum was great. They even scored ten points in a row. As a result, Mei Gong won by 42 to 30. Although Huadong lost, their performance was also very good. It was fate, not a sin of war. The referee was Xu Zhendong.

Free Talk

[P Talks About Liu San Xia Fei

Su Manshu sent Liu San a poem from Baimen: "Thank you Liu San for asking about my news, I still have a faint life to be a poetry monk." Also, a verse about hearing the sound of cuckoos at night in Taoguang Temple, West Lake, sent to Liu San: "Liu San was a passionate seed in the past, wandering in the misty waves for another year." Manshu also made Baimen Autumn Willow Picture, Wenji Picture, and Huangye Tower Picture for Liu San. The friendship between Liu San and Manshu, and Liu San's romantic and unrestrained life, can be seen from this. Liu San, originally named Ji Ping, was from Shanghai, with the pseudonym Jiangnan, and also signed as Jiangnan Liu San. During the Guangxu and Xuantong years, he studied at Chengcheng School of the Army Cavalry Department in Tokyo. He was good at poetry and calligraphy, especially proficient in Han Li. He studied and imitated for more than 30 years, benefiting from Shimen Song. He once lectured at Peking University and jointly revised the example of selling books with Shen Yinmo. For a time, he was famous in the north and south. People scrambled to treasure every inch of his work.

During the Su Bao case, Zhang Taiyan and Zou Rong were detained in prison. Zou Rong died of illness in prison. Lu Yan Changchi dared not ask about it. Liu San calmly and unhurriedly collected the body and buried it next to the Huangye Tower in his hometown of Hua Jing Township. His chivalrous and righteous deeds shone brightly for thousands of years. In the 11th year of the Republic of China, Yu Youren, Zhang Taiyan, Li Yinquan, Zhang Puquan, Zhang Shizhao, and others personally offered sacrifices and erected a monument in his memory. Taiyan wrote the inscription calling him a righteous man, taking the allusion from Gong Ding'an's poem "Liu San is now a righteous man."

Liu has an addiction to things in the cup. His drinking capacity is no less than that of his predecessor Liu Ling. Because it was difficult to find good wine on the market, he made his own. He had to drink at every meal. When he drank to a high level of excitement, he sang loudly. His wife, Lu Lingsu, was knowledgeable and courteous, and especially proficient in Kunqu opera. The husband and wife sang and followed each other, enjoying the ultimate happiness in the world. Liu once gambled with a painter and drank as a game. After the meal, the servant said that today we drank more than 60 catties of wine together. His drinking capacity can be imagined.

His poetic chanting is also very readable. I will record a few chapters to summarize the rest. Remember two poems: "Remember the bright ferry bridge in spring, dressed in crimson to block the road and ask about the morning. For no reason, I took leave to go to Jiangnan, reducing the beauty by an inch of waist." "The orioles fly in disorder in Jiangnan in March. I cut off the Wusong and returned again. I bought a pair of dragon flowers, and the peach blossoms hit my spring clothes like snow." Giving to Lingsu: "The waters of Wan and Xiang are endless, and his tracks are also vertical and horizontal. How can he not finish his soaring intention, and want to travel ten thousand miles to Huanglong." "It is not possible to listen to the absurdities of women. He should look at the old Liu Ling in the mountains and rivers. A drunk man wrongly passed on his family law and willingly served as a makeup table to sue for drunkenness and awakening." Sending Manshu to India: "He indulged in Zen in his early years and saw the truth of nature. The old house in the rivers and mountains is lonely and sad. He suddenly made a plan to go south with the scriptures on his shoulders. The white horse is the second person to invest in the wilderness." All are brilliant verses.

Liu San and Huang Huiwen, Zhu Zhengzhuang, Liu Zaifu, Liu Yazi, Shen

Interesting Interpretation of Idioms · Bing · Xiu

There is a Liang family boy next door, who is erudite, ingenious, and good at eloquence. He once said that many sentences in the "Story Qionglin" book are appropriate for the current situation. For example, "Jingwei carrying stones is compared to people's futile efforts," which refers to Wang Jingwei holding a grudge against Chiang Kai-shek, and comparing the failure of the enlarged meeting to his futile efforts. Also, "Stones from other mountains can be used to attack jade," which refers to Chiang Kai-shek, who forced Yan Xishan to go elsewhere, and can also be used to attack and retreat Feng Yuxiang. Ingenious words and soothing mood, or also the same class as the Eastern Chun Yu. (Que Chou)

Small Records of National Boundaries · Hai · Ke

▲ There are many people in London, the capital of England, who advocate night school. According to a recent survey, there are 10,000 night classes, 8,000 teachers, and 250,000 students.

▲ The famous luxury car in the United States has all kinds of extremely exquisite and comfortable equipment, equipped with wireless electricity to receive the latest market conditions. Now this car has been destroyed, and those who hear it feel sorry for it.

▲ There is a goldfish in the small pool of a hotel in London that has lived for 30 years. It can be regarded as the longest-lived goldfish. It has now been moved to a hotel in Brighton for maintenance.

▲ Darlington, Stockton, Yarm, and Schildn are said to be the birthplace of British railways. A centenary celebration was held, which was very grand.

▲ A film reel of Queen Victoria of England's last visit to Dublin, the capital of Ireland, has a lot of historical interest and is currently being kept by a British gentleman as a treasure.

▲ All photos and statues of the former abolished emperor in public places in Germany have been completely removed or dismantled since the end of the European War and the collapse of the royal family.

▲ The famous British drama "Money Tons" was sent to major theaters after the writer compiled it, asking for rehearsals, but they were all rejected. Later, a theater bought it at a low price, rehearsed it, and performed it, which was very popular with the public. The income in London alone was as much as 120,000 gold pounds.

Yinmo, Chen Zhongfu, Ma Yichu, Zhang Puquan, etc. were friends in poetry and prose.

Recently, he was appointed as a member of the Supervisory Committee of the Supervisory Yuan. Some people do not know who he is. Describe this as an introduction.

Ode to the Snow Elephant Pu

It has been snowing continuously for days and has not cleared. The amount of snow is unprecedented in the past 30 years. The light cold makes people feel shivering and pitiful, but those who are drinking happily around the stove and sleeping comfortably under the quilt often take this as a joke. A few days ago, my friend Mr. Gu Xuchu built a Buddha statue, like a Bodhisattva lowering his eyebrows, hollow in the middle, with an electric lamp running through it, supported by a table, about three feet high. In the evening, the background was entrusted to a black curtain, and photographer Wang Kai next to the County Temple was called to make several photos, which were distributed to like-minded people, which was also a refined and leisurely interest. And my neighbor has built a beautiful woman statue with accumulated snow, which is especially a charm of boudoir people. I have already appreciated it, and there must be words. Therefore, I write a few words below.

▲ Snow Maitreya Flying tin came to visit, the earth returned to spring, thousands of worlds, carved jade and piled silver. Awakening infatuated dreams, washing away the mundane world. Occasionally showing the color phase, changing the shape and separating the body. Cold is not poor, the chest has an ice heart. Opening the face to preach the Dharma, the result comes from the cause. The setting sun shines westward, and the rise and fall exceed the beauty. The empty mountain and flowing water begin to return to the truth.

▲ Snow Beauty Qionglou Yexiao, Qiong girl makes incense, Gu She's graceful appearance, plain and white dress. Talented Yongxu, ice and snow heart. The life experience of flying flowers is still sad. Yu Yun Kong remembers, three lives dream long. Even if there is romance, half of the face remains. Ask Vimo, why stay in the stream of fragrance. Such immortal companions are hard to hide in a golden house.

A Record of Snow on Gushan Mountain to Find Plum Blossoms

He Haisheng sent from Hangzhou

A few days ago, spring snow was flying, day and night. The white Yuqiong Building in Hangzhou has become a silver world. West Lake is also very colorful. The beauty of nature is more believable than artificial art.

I could endure the cold, so I invited Lu and Zhai to go to West Lake to play in the snow. When we arrived at the lake, there were no boats. The high mountains were covered with snow, like wearing white fur. Thin ice floats on the surface of the water, and the wind is slightly rippling. Zhai wanted to go to Gushan Mountain to find plum blossoms. Lu was healthy enough to walk directly to the place. We drank tea at Gushan Tea House. The plums are divided into five colors: big red, pink, green, white, and yellow. Snow accumulates on the branches, and they all look white from a distance. The jade bones and ice muscles are ethereal and immortal. It is appropriate for the hermit Lin to love it like a wife. I improvised a poem: "The empty pavilion is silent at the foot of Gushan Mountain. Jade bones and ice muscles, thousands of trees and plums. Ask the romantic hermit Lin, can the crane come back when the moon is bright?" We visited the tomb of hermit Lin. There is a crane tomb next to it, both covered with snow. His pure breeze and bright festival can be imagined as his person. The three of us mourned in the snow for a long time, and all envied his pile of yellow [blank], which has remained famous for thousands of years, and will be immortal with West Lake.

We sat and walked back to the lake. We had dinner at Juxian Pavilion. It was nine o'clock when we returned home. (Que Chou)

Qing Dynasty Talk in the Book World Countryman

Tang Zailiang, who lectured on Romance of the Three Kingdoms, is also a backbone member of the Guangyu Society. It was originally scheduled to work with Shen Jian'an and Xue Xiaoqing, who sang and played the Pearl Tower, on the 17th of the lunar calendar. During the day, he opened a book in Qunyulou, and in the evening, he opened a book in Chunfeng Deyilou on the same day. However, Shen and Xue had a very close friendship with Wang Yunfeng, who lectured on Jinqiang Fu. Therefore, they openly declared that they were unwilling to cooperate with Tang, and waited for Tang to choose himself. If Tang did Qunyulou day and night, Shen, Xue, and Wang would do Deyilou. If Tang decided to do Deyilou, Shen and the other three would do Qunyu. If Tang wanted to do both places day and night, Shen and the others would not do one place. However, the owners of the two venues both held the bear's paw and fish at the same time, and they were unwilling to give in. Later, Zhu Yaoting and others tried to mediate and focused on the four words "suitable for people and places." They probably persuaded Tang to do Qunyu alone, and Deyilou would be taken over by Shen and the other three.

The Great World Amusement Park still plans to add a book venue and invite Zhao Xiaoqing, Zhao Hesun, and others to take over. According to legend, on the evening of February 14, Xiaoqing's father and son's residence (Guianli, Glock Road, French Concession) was suddenly robbed and robbed of clothes, jewelry, etc., worth about four or five hundred gold. Xiaoqing did not know the legal procedures, so he did not report the arrest and ask for arrest. It is not easy to live in Chang'an. Really. (Unstamped)

Tobacco Ridicule Ji Jin

Tobacco has no benefits to hygiene. However, everyone likes it. In recent times, the sales market has become wider day by day. And Virginia in North America has become the center of the world's tobacco. According to legend, before Columbus arrived in America, the people of Europe and the West did not smoke at all. I don’t know what tobacco is. Since Mr. Ke returned, a shipowner named Lailai brought him home. One day, he tried to sit alone and smoke it. His servant was serving the basin to enter. Seeing the smoke coming out of the master's mouth and nose, he thought it was fire. He was shocked. Before he could call for help, he poured the water from the basin and poured it on his head. Mr. Lai didn't know why he was soaked thoroughly. Really a fun story.

Since tobacco was imported into Europe, the whole country has been smoking hard. Almost without this gentleman for a day. And Virginia's supply fell short of demand. Therefore, the countries of Jiqian Di, Beikal Le, and Nadiev Foss also developed land and widely planted. Seed in early spring and ripen in late autumn. Harvest and bake it dry. Carried to the market. In total, the annual production should reach US$2,640 trillion. One-third of them are distributed in the Americas and two-thirds in Europe and Asia. The number is also huge.

Since tobacco is a pastime for civilized people, I don’t know that it contains a lot of toxins. The so-called nicotine. According to a Westerner, one English mile can kill two or three people. Fortunately, half of it is burned off when it is burned and smoked. However, the harm is also not small. We are working hard writing, with a cigarette in hand. It is said that it can help grow literary thoughts. It seems that we have never felt any impact. By the time we are older and the energy is already weak, we gradually develop chronic carbon poisoning, which is incurable. This is what those who study hygiene should pay attention to.

▲ Short News The dancer Ms. Violet. Good at Beijing and Cantonese opera, her name shook the north and south. Recently, in the Nanjing Road Municipal Hall, a united collection of famous ladies from the pavilion, and the stars of the brother and dance, sold very well. Programs such as Spring is Deep, Mandarin Ducks Playing in the Water, Crescent Moon, Peach and Plum Competing for Spring, Dragon and Tiger Fighting, Selling Flower Words, Butterfly Girl, Innocence, Flower of Love. Ms. Chen Miaochang's Cantonese opera, Beijing opera sitting in the palace, Suzhou ditty, comedy Half Chicken, toe dance, Violet Dance, etc. are all masterpieces. (Rui Hongchu)

South Seas Travelogue (123) - Flowers

Most travelers to Siam are from Chaozhou, Guangdong. There are also Jiangzhe Guild Halls. There was once a carpenter who, due to his carpentry skills in construction, gained the trust of the Siamese King, leading to great wealth. This was because the former Siamese King appreciated the beauty of engineering and did not haggle over prices. However, Siamese workers are not like that now; they calculate everything carefully before proceeding. The Siamese King is young and studied in England, so he can speak English. However, he appointed a certain Chinese gentleman to manage Chinese Buddhist affairs, even though he is not well-versed in Buddhism, simply because he can speak Siamese.

Besides commerce, the industries of Chinese living abroad are also noteworthy. There are many Luban Temples in various places. Siam, Burma, and India all have remarkable woodworking industries, mostly run by people from Guangdong. In northern Burma, some have become wealthy by contracting civil engineering projects. One gentleman initially handled clerical work with a monthly income of only one hundred yuan but made tens of thousands within two years by contracting work as a foreman for a British company. There is a type of woodworking where Chinese are earning a lot of money from the Japanese. Everywhere in Japan, we see the Japanese using fine redwood furniture, all the time. Small tables and Buddhist altars are especially common. Formerly, it was thought to be produced in Japan, but later it was known to be entirely made by Chinese. The wood comes from the South Seas, and the manufacturing takes place in Guangdong and Shanghai, making it a major Chinese export. Furthermore, ivory, lapis lazuli, jade, and other materials are produced in Siam and Burma. Chinese merchants transport them to Shanghai and Guangdong, where Chinese workers craft them into various utensils for export to Europe and America. From this, it can be seen that Chinese craftsmanship is naturally developed. It is a pity that they do not know how to improve.

On the 12th, I visited Mr. Liu Guangsu's sawmill on Vinton Street. It uses machinery for sawing and has a capital of 200,000 yuan. According to him, business has declined by about seven or eight times compared to the past. Examining the reasons, part of it is due to the impact of Gandhi's anti-British movement. Indians do not use any machinery, and construction has come to a standstill. Gandhi is a restorationist who uses methods that go backward and overthrow commercial policies. In Burma, there are quite a few Chinese sawmills, mostly run by Cantonese people. A certain Mr. Li and his brothers are engaged in this business. According to him, there are three types of Burmese wood. The first type is Xian wood, also called Mali, or Teak. This wood is the most durable and the most expensive and indispensable for shipbuilding because it is resistant to collisions. The largest sales are to Britain, mainly for shipbuilding, especially for warships. I think that as long as the world does not cease war for a day, the best materials will be sacrificed for war. The next best is Ding Sha wood, or Eng. The next is red wood, or Ponkato (transliteration of Burmese). These woods all come from northern Burma, but they are not the same as the red wood used in Guangdong furniture. They are very suitable for railway sleepers. Mr. Li said that all construction wood in China should be transported from Burma. However, I have visited a Japanese sawmill company in the three eastern provinces with a capital of one million, and I know that the eastern provinces are not lacking in large timber, but it is a pity that it has not been transported out.

On the 20th, I received a letter from Liu Tingbi of the Pengcheng Liu Clan Association in Bassein, requesting me to write a couplet for the Pengcheng Liu Clan. I had long wanted to go to the countryside to learn about local customs, so I replied by telegram, indicating that I would arrive at the Pengcheng Guild Hall immediately. I boarded the ship at 4 PM, second class for nine yuan. There were absolutely no amenities, the electric fan was not working, and the room could not even accommodate a table. Strangely, there was no shower. So, it cost three times as much for nothing. Ordinary class costs less than three yuan. The second class on these ships is not as spacious as a train. I met a black Indian who spoke English very well. We debated briefly, and he strongly advocated for racial equality and intermarriage. He then said with emotion, "I am but a slave, with no right to speak." Along the river, I saw a lot of duckweed, floating in the water in large groups, which was very beautiful. Occasionally, in the setting sun, the golden pagodas and green trees reflected each other, which is a beautiful scene of Burma. The ship sailed southwest, and there were many large factories across the river from Yangon.

On the morning of the 21st, Liu Dongxian (also known as Tingbi) and many members of the Liu clan were waiting at the station to greet me. We took a car to the Pengcheng Guild Hall, which had two elementary schools. It is said that there are several hundred Liu families here. Dongxian's mother was Burmese, and his father was from Anxi, Fujian. He returned to China at the age of fifteen and graduated from the Business Department of China University in Beijing. He stayed in China for eighteen years before returning to Burma. His mother passed away long ago, but he still enjoys the Burmese scenery. I came to Bassein and stayed with Liu at Liu Wenjian's Quan Yuan business. Liu is the director of the Pengcheng Guild Hall. That evening, the guild hall hosted a banquet. There were not many Liu family members present because most of them were in the countryside. After dinner, we took a car to tour various parts of Bassein. There is an aircraft factory to the north, as well as Catholic and Jesus churches. Bassein is the largest famous port in the southwest corner of Burma. It can be seen on the map, located between India and the South Seas, connecting to India. Large European and American ships can sail directly into the inner harbor. Rice is the main commercial commodity. In the past, the British wanted to establish their capital here instead of Yangon, but it did not happen, which shows its importance. Bassein is written as Pathein on the map.

Guidelines for Submissions to the Art World

(1) Text: Limited to news, reviews, and introductions of the latest art (music, engraving, architecture, drama, etc.) and literature, both domestic and foreign.

(2) Photos: Limited to recent portraits of domestic and foreign artists, their works, and various photographs related to the text.

(3) The length of each text should not exceed 2,000 characters.

(5) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

Manuscripts should be written horizontally and neatly, avoiding abbreviations in Western languages. If it is necessary to quote original text, it must be attached below the translation.

(7) Do not use blueprints or colored paper for illustrations attached to the manuscript. Use white paper with black ink.

(8) Please address submissions to the "Art World Editorial Department."

(9) Submissions will not be returned, whether published or not. If you require a return, please state this in advance and include sufficient postage.

(10) Remuneration for text is divided into three levels: four yuan, three yuan, or two yuan per thousand characters. The same applies to drawings and photos per piece. Special submissions will be remunerated separately.

[Youth Corner]

First Place: Bai Wan

The exams are almost over.

There is only one subject left, which doesn't require preparation or studying, and can be taken with the exam. Therefore, most students are sitting in their dorms chatting. Judging from their tired expressions and sleepless eyes, the exams have left a severe and terrible impression on them. They must have suffered a lot and spent a lot of effort for it. So, in this moment of near completion, they are like workers who have put down a heavy load to rest. Everyone is relieved, and their hearts feel much happier and more relaxed.

The scope of their conversations in the dorm at this time,

is probably nothing more than how not to easily let go of this winter vacation, and how to compensate for the fatigue and loss of playtime suffered during the preparation for the exams. Some are talking about how happy it will be to sit around with their older and younger sisters and mothers at home, spending the Lunar New Year. Students who have no home to return to are discussing inviting a few classmates to organize a winter vacation accommodation for students staying on campus, preparing to make their lives artistic and interesting. They rarely talk about the exam questions this time, because this matter is considered past, and talking about it is too boring, or it will make them angry. There are always a few students who regret in their hearts that they answered a certain exam question incorrectly, or are jealous that others got first place and they failed.

"Hey, talking about these advance pleasures is meaningless. I have a suggestion, which is to make the atmosphere at this moment happy and interesting. Do you agree?"

At this time, Lin, who was sitting quietly like a child, suddenly jumped up and said this.

"Good, I second it," said Qiong, nicknamed "Sharp-Mouth," echoing.

"My suggestion is..." Jing pulled the corner of Lin's clothes, meaning to stop her from speaking. Lin herself smiled at Fen, who was sitting in the east corner of the dorm, lost in thought.

"Speak, hurry up and speak," Sharp-Mouth urged.

"I won't say it, alas, it's too pitiful. If I say it in a moment, I'm afraid I'll cry," Lin said, stopping after hearing Jing's instructions.

"No, saying half a sentence like this will shorten your life and leave us all confused," said someone named Ying. Sharp-Mouth got up and pulled Lin, insisting that she had to speak.

"Okay, I'll say it," Lin finally said, her eyes never leaving Fen. "My suggestion is that we are too bored sitting here doing nothing. Why not think of a way to get some money, buy something, and have a meal together?"

"Where's the way?" asked Li, the famous king of good food, hurriedly.

"The way is," Lin looked at Fen and smiled, "whoever is the first place in this exam, invites everyone."

"Good, good..."

"Agree, agree..."

It seemed everyone was looking at Fen, because Fen got the most points in this exam.

"Now let's examine who is the first place in our exam this time," Ying said deliberately.

"Besides Fen, who else? Isn't she the first in every subject?" Sharp-Mouth said directly.

"Then, please our first-place Fen quickly sacrifice a few dollars to treat us," said Li, the king of good food.

"Fen, take out the money and treat us," everyone said.

At this time, Fen said calmly, "Okay, a few dollars is nothing, but I don't have a single cent right now, I'll treat you another day, okay?"

"No, no, we want to eat right now."

"If you don't have money, I'll lend it to you."

Everyone surrounded Fen, insisting that she take out the money immediately, but Fen insisted on not agreeing.

"Hey, you all don't know how to handle things," said Jing, who had first stopped Lin from making the proposal. "If you want someone to treat, you have to give them gifts and congratulations first, and then worry about them not taking out the money."

The school will assign mentors to athletes based on their subjects. This mentor will be with the students day and night, reviewing the material they did not understand in the lecture hall, or the material they missed due to absence. The mentor will explain the exercises in the material to the athlete, making sure they fully understand the difficulties. Before the exam, the mentor will fully present the important points of the entire book, allowing the student to review it so they can pass the exam. This measure by the school provides much help to the athletes' academics, ensuring that their exam scores will not be too poor. In the future, they can also apply what they have learned to serve society. According to the principal of the school, the athletes sacrifice their academics for the school, which is pitiful. If they are not given remediation, their grades will be too poor, and they will not be able to graduate. If they are casually promoted and graduated, the school rules do not allow it, so this method was established. Most of the mentors are recent graduates of the school.

Dedicated to Miss X Who is About to Marry - Shi Yi

The cold and severe weather is blowing a fierce wind that scrapes the skin, immersed in this gray atmosphere, making people feel cold and shudder. Many friends are huddling by the warm stove to roast fire, but I am alone at my desk, writing this blessing to a friend.

Girl, I was once a good friend of yours. During the period at X University, you were praised by the male students as the so-called university flower. You were the modern lady who caused a sensation throughout the school. Girl, you were so charming at that time, so beautiful, with soft hair draped over your shoulders, revealing a round apple-like delicate face. Two lively eyes that seemed about to roll out seemed to contain infinite affection.

Thin lips often revealed pearly white teeth, wearing a Chinese-Western fusion cheongsam, high-heeled leather shoes, making the students willingly surrender beneath your pomegranate skirt. At that time, you were also rich in poetic talent and were called a female poet. Your gorgeous image could often be seen on Xima Road, and you were a smart and lively girl, firmly believing in being a social butterfly. I can recall many things here from my memories.

In your dormitory, there were often friends from afar who yearned for the saint, especially the students from our school. I remember your bedroom was a small square room with artistic wallpaper, movie posters, and various colored paper flowers. In one corner of the wall was a bed with iron bars, red, green, and beautiful bedding. In the middle was a writing desk with many decorations, so that no one who had been there did not praise your bedroom. "Miss X, you are truly gifted with intelligence, rich in artistic talent. You can arrange such an ordinary room so exquisitely." Another person would continue, "Miss X's literature is very good. Don't you see the poems that are often published in the Central Daily News?" At that time, you were very proud to receive the awards from your classmates. Girl, in the past, you were worth being proud of in a very glorious page in your life history.

I recently heard good news that in the near future, you will encounter a happy day. You will be wearing light and flowing scarlet georgette, beautiful and fashionable clothing, holding the hand of your groom in the auditorium. You, this passionate girl, are giving your girlish pure love to him for the sake of loving him. For this, Miss X, who is about to marry, before you marry, I want to sincerely bless you and tell you, do not forget how fortunate and glorious you were in your past life. I hope that the gentle and red brilliance of your life will always shine like the sun and moon. I hope that your beautiful youth will always be stored in the rose garden, surrounded by the waters of spring, forever preserving the vivid flowers. I also pray that my friend will seek a line of light in the women's world, and that you will present people's songs of joy among female writers. With the sincerity of your love, may you always preserve happiness in the world. With the passion of your love, may you build a great career in the future. Girl, the short words of blessing you see are some light gifts flowing from my heart to you. Do not forget that she was once a close companion on the island of friendship in the past, and she sincerely blesses you in a corner of West Shanghai.

Guidelines for Book and Newspaper Review Submissions

(1) Text: Limited to reviews of the latest domestic and foreign publications. In addition to literary works, all political, economic, legal, scientific, educational, etc., books and newspapers are eligible for review, but unrelated books and newspapers will not be reviewed.

(2) Drawings: Limited to recent works by new domestic and foreign artists and illustrations related to the text.

(3) Texts on textual research or research on ancient Chinese books will not be published.

(4) Drawings and photos must be related to the text.

(5) The length of each text should not exceed 3,000 characters.

(6) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(7) Do not use blueprints for drawings, and do not use colored paper. Use white paper with black ink.

(8) Please address submissions to the "Women's Life Editorial Department."

(9) Submissions will not be returned, whether published or not. If you require a return, please state this in advance and include sufficient postage.

(10) Remuneration for text is divided into three levels: three yuan, two yuan, or one yuan per thousand characters. The same applies to drawings and photos per piece. Special submissions will be remunerated separately.

Social News

Marshal Foch's War Diary (Continued) - Translated by Gu Angruo

The Second Army gradually regained its confidence. Duchesne arrived and had a better effect. The army no longer talked about retreat. Retreat was something I explicitly forbade. The cavalry did not have enough courage.

Whenever you need me, I can return to Romilly. However, my troops here have not yet been deployed and have not yet resumed their advance, so I cannot leave. Our war zone is very wide, from Dinsèque to La Laire and Noon, so many unexpected accidents are possible. Foch.

Furthermore, if you and General Franchet d'Espèrey agree, I propose that our left wing (the Tenth Army) advance from La Laire towards the Scheldt River, with Don, Armentières and Vaux as its target. The British army advances to the north of La Laire, forming a line from Don to Coura Laire. In this way, the French, British, and Belgian detachments can form a line on the left bank of the Scheldt River and the Lys River.

Because Commander-in-Chief Franchet d'Espèrey hoped that on October 10th, a corps (the Second Corps) and two cavalry divisions would engage between Baizain and Aire, and on October 12th, the Third Corps and two cavalry divisions would engage between Baizain and Saint-Omer, we prepared on the 10th to immediately attack and clear the line. The details of the arrangement are as follows:

Under the current situation of the Allied forces, the first thing to do is to carefully complete the union of the British and French armies. The Allied forces have been dispersed by the recent battles.

The area north and east of La Laire, between the Scheldt and Lys rivers, seems to be a suitable battlefield for this operation.

If tomorrow, the 11th, and the day after tomorrow, the 12th, the left wing of the French Tenth Army receives the assistance of the British army (the 200th Regiment and divisions), and can fight on the Baizain-Merville line, then the road to La Laire can be expected to be cleared.

On the other hand, it seems that there are no heavy troops stationed in the northern area of the Merville-Hazebrouck-Cassel line (which is our defense area). Under this situation, on the morning of the 13th, the left wing of the French army can confidently advance towards La Laire, and then towards Don. The right wing of the British army advances towards the area north of La Laire, and then towards Nieuport. The center of the British army advances towards Coura Laire.

By controlling the Scheldt River with Don and the Lys River with Coura Laire, the British, French, and Belgian troops can leisurely meet behind the two rivers.

If the commander-in-chief of the British army agrees to these plans, the French army can act on the Oustre-Esterve-Aitun-Van Gier-Berzie-La Laire-Don route and the southern route. The British army can use the northern route. Please approve the above plan. Foch.

Sir Franchet d'Espèrey was quite able to assist the French army with all his strength and speed, but due to the delay in disembarking, the first division of the British Third Corps did not gather until the afternoon of the 13th, and the entire army was not ready to advance until the evening of the 15th. (To be continued)
